              qualityPromptActive = false;\n84\t            }\n85\t        }\n86\t    }\n87\t\n88\t    /**\n89\t     * Show a quality degradation prompt card\n90\t     */\n91\t    function showQualityPrompt(link) {\n92\t        // Use consistent linkID computation (matches monitorLinkQuality)\n93\t        const linkID = link.link_id || (link.node_mac + ':' + link.peer_mac);\n94\t\n95\t        // Check if already dismissed today\n96\t        const today = new Date().toDateString();\n97\t        const dismissKey = `${linkID}_${today}`;\n98\t        if (dismissedQualityPrompts.has(dismissKey)) {\n99\t            return;\n100\t        }\n101\t\n102\t        qualityPromptActive = true;\n103\t\n104\t        const linkName = link.name || formatLinkID(linkID);\n105\t        const qualityPercent = Math.round((link.composite_score || link.quality || 0) * 100);\n106\t\n107\t        // Remove existing prompt if present\n108\t        const <p class=\"quality-prompt-detail\">This link is experiencing degraded performance, which may affect detection accuracy in this area.</p>\n125\t            </div>\n126\t            <div class=\"quality-prompt-actions\">\n127\t                <button class=\"quality-prompt-btn quality-prompt-diagnose\" onclick=\"Proactive.diagnoseLink('${linkID}')\">\n128\t                    <span to document\n137\t        document.body.appendChild(prompt);\n138\t\n139\t        // Highlight the 3D link line if available\n140\t        highlightLinkIn3D(linkID);\n141\t    }\n142\t\n143\t    /**\n144\t     * Dismiss the current quality prompt\n145\t     */\n146\t    function dismissQualityPrompt() {\n147\t        qualityPromptActive = false;\n148\t        qualityPromptLinkID = null;\n149\t        qualityPromptStartTime = null;\n150\t\n151\t        const prompt = document.getElementById('quality-prompt-card');\n152\t        if (prompt) {\n153\t            prompt.remove();\n154\t        }\n155\t\n156\t        // Remove link highlight\n157\t        unhighlightLinkIn3D();\n158\t    }\n159\t\n160\t    /**\n161\t     * Dismiss the quality prompt for today only\n162\t     */\n163\t    function dismissQualityPromptForToday() {\n164\t        if (qualityPromptLinkID) {\n165\t            const today = new Date().toDateString();\n166\t            const dismissKey = `${qualityPromptLinkID}_${today}`;\n167\t            dismissedQualityPrompts.add(dismissKey);\n168\t\n169\t            // Persist to localStorage\n170\t            try {\n171\t                const dismissed = Array.from(dismissedQualityPrompts);\n172\t                localStorage.setItem('spaxel_dismissed_quality_prompts', dismissed.join(','));\n173\t            } catch (e) {\n174\t                console.warn('Failed to save dismissed prompts:', e);\n175\t            }\n176\t        }\n177\t\n178\t        dismissQualityPrompt();\n179\t    }\n180\t\n181\t    /**\n182\t     * Load dismissed prompts from localStorage\n183\t     */\n184\t    function loadDismissedPrompts() {\n185\t        try {\n186\t            const saved = localStorage.getItem('spaxel_dismissed_quality_prompts');\n187\t            if (saved) {\n188\t                const today = new Date().toDateString();\n189\t                const all = saved.split(',').filter(id => id);\n190\t                // Only keep today's entries to prevent stale data buildup\n191\t                dismissedQualityPrompts = new Set(all.filter(key => key.endsWith(today)));\n192\t            }\n193\t        } catch (e) {\n194\t            console.warn('Failed to load dismissed prompts:', e);\n195\t        }\n196\t    }\n197\t\n198\t    /**\n199\t     * Highlight a link in the 3D view with pulsing amber animation\n200\t     */\n201\t    function highlightLinkIn3D(linkID) {\n202\t        // Store original state before highlighting\n203\t        if (window.Viz3D && window.Viz3D.forEachLink) {\n204\t            window.Viz3D.forEachLink(function(line, id) {\n205\t                if (id === linkID && !line.userData.originalState) {\n206\t                    // Store original material state\n207\t                    line.userData.originalState = {\n208\t                        opacity: line.material.opacity,\n209\t                        transparent: line.material.transparent,\n210\t                        color: line.material.color ? line.material.color.getHex() : null,\n211\t                        emissiveColor: line.material.emissive ? line.material.emissive.getHex() : undefined,\n212\t                        emissiveIntensity: line.material.emissive ? line.material.emissiveIntensity : 0\n213\t                    };\n214\t                }\n215\t            });\n216\t        }\n217\t\n218\t        // Use Viz3D highlightLink with amber color (0xff9800) and emissive glow\n219\t        if (window.Viz3D && window.Viz3D.highlightLink) {\n220\t            window.Viz3D.highlightLink(linkID, 0xff9800, 0xff9800, 0.5);\n221\t        }\n222\t\n223\t        // Dispatch custom event\n224\t        window.dispatchEvent(new CustomEvent('spaxel:highlight-link', {\n225\t            detail: { linkID: linkID, highlight: true, pulsing: true }\n226\t        }));\n227\t\n228\t        // Start pulsing animation for this link\n229\t        startLinkPulsing(linkID);\n230\t    }\n231\t\n232\t    /**\n233\t     * Remove link highlight in 3D view\n234\t     */\n235\t    function unhighlightLinkIn3D() {\n236\t        const linkID = qualityPromptLinkID;\n237\t\n238\t        if (linkID && window.Viz3D) {\n239\t            // Restore the link's original appearance using Viz3D's restore mechanism\n240\t            if (window.Viz3D.forEachLink) {\n241\t                window.Viz3D.forEachLink(function(line, id) {\n242\t                    if (id === linkID && line.userData.originalState) {\n243\t                        const orig = line.userData.originalState;\n244\t                        line.material.opacity = orig.opacity;\n245\t                        line.material.transparent = orig.transparent;\n246\t                        if (line.material.color && orig.color !== null) {\n247\t                            line.material.color.setHex(orig.color);\n248\t                        }\n249\t                        if (line.material.emissive) {\n250\t                            line.material.emissiveIntensity = orig.emissiveIntensity || 0;\n251\t                            if (orig.emissiveColor !== undefined) {\n252\t                                line.material.emissive.setHex(orig.emissiveColor);\n253\t                            }\n254\t                        }\n255\t                        line.material.needsUpdate = true;\n256\t                    }\n257\t                });\n258\t            }\n259\t\n260\t            window.dispatchEvent(new CustomEvent('spaxel:highlight-link', {\n261\t                detail: { linkID: linkID, highlight: false }\n262\t            }));\n263\t        }\n264\t\n265\t        // Stop pulsing animation\n266\t        stopLinkPulsing();\n267\t    }\n268\t\n269\t    /**\n270\t     * Start pulsing animation for a highlighted link\n271\t     */\n272\t    function startLinkPulsing(linkID) {\n273\t        // Stop any existing animation\n274\t        stopLinkPulsing();\n275\t\n276\t        pulseTime = 0;\n277\t        const PULSE_CYCLE = 1.5; // 1.5 second pulse cycle\n278\t\n279\t        function animatePulse(timestamp) {\n280\t            if (!qualityPromptActive || qualityPromptLinkID !== linkID) {\n281\t                return; // Stop animation\n282\t            }\n283\t\n284\t            if (!pulsingAnimationID) {\n285\t                pulsingAnimationID = requestAnimationFrame(animatePulse);\n286\t                return;\n287\t            }\n288\t\n289\t            pulseTime += 0.016; // Approximately 60fps\n290\t\n291\t            // Calculate pulse phase (0 to 1)\n292\t            const phase = (pulseTime % PULSE_CYCLE) / PULSE_CYCLE;\n293\t\n294\t            // Opacity oscillates: 0.3 -> 0.8 -> 0.3\n295\t            const intensity = 0.3 + 0.5 * (1 - Math.abs(phase - 0.5) * 2);\n296\t\n297\t            // Apply pulsing effect to link\n298\t            if (window.Viz3D && window.Viz3D.highlightLink) {\n299\t                // Vary the emissive intensity for pulsing glow effect\n300\t                const baseIntensity = 0.3;\n301\t                const pulseIntensity = baseIntensity + (0.7 * intensity);\n302\t                window.Viz3D.highlightLink(linkID, 0xff9800, 0xff9800, pulseIntensity);\n303\t            }\n304\t\n305\t            pulsingAnimationID = requestAnimationFrame(animatePulse);\n306\t        }\n307\t\n308\t        pulsingAnimationID = requestAnimationFrame(animatePulse);\n309\t    }\n310\t\n311\t    /**\n312\t     * Stop the link pulsing animation\n313\t     */\n314\t    function stopLinkPulsing() {\n315\t        if (pulsingAnimationID) {\n316\t            cancelAnimationFrame(pulsingAnimationID);\n317\t            pulsingAnimationID = null;\n318\t        }\n319\t        pulseTime = 0;\n320\t    }\n321\t\n322\t    /**\n323\t     * Run diagnostics for a link and show results\n324\t     */\n325\t    function diagnoseLink(linkID) {\n326\t        // Fetch diagnostic results from API\n327\t        fetch(`/api/diagnostics/link/${encodeURIComponent(linkID)}`)\n328\t            .then(res => res.json())\n329\t            .then(data => {\n330\t                showDiagnosticResults(linkID, data);\n331\t            })\n332\t            .catch(err => {\n333\t                console.error('Failed to fetch diagnostics:', err);\n334\t                showDiagnosticError(linkID);\n335\t            });\n336\t    }\n337\t\n338\t    /**\n339\t     * Show diagnostic results in a slide-out panel\n340\t     */\n341\t    function showDiagnosticResults(linkID, response) {\n342\t        // Remove  // Handle both old format (diagnosis array) and new format (response with diagnosis + health)\n353\t        const diagnosis = response.diagnosis || response[0] || {};\n354\t        const health = response.health || diagnosis.health || null;\n355\t        const hasDiagnosis = diagnosis.title !== undefined;\n356\t        const severity = (diagnosis.severity || <span class=\"diagnostic-link-id\">${formatLinkID(linkID)}</span>\n367\t                </div>\n368\t\n369\t                ${hasDiagnosis ? `\n370\t                    <div class=\"diagnostic-result diagnostic-severity-${severity}\">\n371\t                        <div class=\"diagnostic-result-title\">${diagnosis.title}</div>\n372\t                        <div    function renderHealthMetrics(health) {\n430\t        if (!health) {\n431\t            return '';\n432\t        }\n433\t\n434\t        // Handle both snapshot format and report format\n435\t     return `\n442\t            <div class=\"health-metric\">\n443\t                <span class=\"metric-label\">Packet Rate:</span>\n444\t                <span class=\"metric-value\">${typeof Detection =====\n468\t\n469\t    /**\n470\t     * Track a settings change for repeated-change detection\n471\t     */\n472\t    function trackSettingChange(settingKey, settingValue) {\n473\t        if (!QUALIFYING_SETTINGS.has(settingKey)) {\n474\t            return; // Not a qualifying setting\n475\t        }\n476\t\n477\t        const now = Date.now();\n478\t        const windowMs = 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000; // 24 hours\n479\t\n480\t        // Initialize history for this setting if needed\n481\t        if (!settingChangeHistory[settingKey]) {\n482\t            settingChangeHistory[settingKey] = [];\n483\t        }\n484\t\n485\t        // Add new change\n486\t        settingChangeHistory[settingKey].push({\n487\t            timestamp: now,\n488\t            value: settingValue\n489\t        });\n490\t\n491\t        // Remove old changes outside the 24h window\n492\t        const cutoff = now - windowMs;\n493\t        settingChangeHistory[settingKey] = settingChangeHistory[settingKey].filter(\n494\t            change => change.timestamp > cutoff\n495\t        );\n496\t\n497\t        // Save to localStorage\n498\t        saveSettingHistory();\n499\t\n500\t        // Check if we should show a hint\n501\t        checkSettingChangeHint(settingKey);\n502\t    }\n503\t\n504\t    /**\n505\t     * Check if a setting change hint should be shown\n506\t     */\n507\t    function checkSettingChangeHint(settingKey) {\n508\t        // Check if hint was already shown for this setting\n509\t        if (settingChangeHintShown[settingKey]) {\n510\t            const lastShown = settingChangeHintShown[settingKey];\n511\t            const cooldownMs = 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000; // 24 hour cooldown\n512\t            if (Date.now() - lastShown < cooldownMs) {\n513\t                return; // Still in cooldown\n514\t            }\n515\t        }\n516\t\n517\t        const changes = settingChangeHistory[settingKey] || [];\n518\t        if (changes.length >= 3) {\n519\t            // Show the hint\n520\t            showSettingChangeHint(settingKey);\n521\t            settingChangeHintShown[settingKey] = Date.now();\n522\t            saveSettingHintShown();\n523\t        }\n524\t    }\n525\t\n526\t    /**\n527\t     * Show a hint for repeated setting changes\n528\t     */\n529\t    function showSettingChangeHint(settingKey) {\n530\t        const settingName = formatSettingName(settingKey);\n531\t\n532\t        // Remove existing hint if present\n533\t        const existing = document.getElementById('setting-change-hint');\n534\t        if (existing) {\n535\t            existing.remove();\n536\t        }\n537\t\n538\t        const hint = `;\n559\t\n560\t        document.body.appendChild(hint);\n561\t    }\n562\t\n563\t    /**\n564\t     * Dismiss the setting change hint\n565\t     */\n566\t    function dismissSettingHint() {\n567\t        const hint = document.getElementById('setting-change-hint');\n568\t        if (hint) {\n569\t            hint.remove();\n570\t        }\n571\t    }\n572\t\n573\t    /**\n574\t     * Start the                 <h3>Analyzing your space...</h3>\n692\t                    <p>Collecting diurnal baseline data and link health metrics to calculate the optimal value.</p>\n693\t                </div>\n694\t            `,\n695\t\n696\t            suggestion: `\n697\t                <div class=\"calibration-step\">\n698\t                    <div class=\"calibration-icon\">✨</div>\n699\t                    <h3>Here's my recommendation</h3>\n700\t                    <div class=\"calibration-suggestion\">\n701\t                        <div class=\"suggestion-value\">\n702\t                            <span class=\"suggestion-label\">Suggested ${formatSettingName(settingKey)}:</span>\n703\t                            <span class=\"suggestion-number\" id=\"suggested-value\">--</span>\n704\t                        </div>\n705\t                        <div class=\"suggestion-reason\" id=\"suggestion-reason\">\n706\t                            Calculating...\n707\t                        </div>\n708\t                    </div>\n709\t                    <div class=\"calibration-metrics\" id=\"calibration-metrics\">\n710\t                        <!-- Metrics will be populated -->\n711\t                    </div>\n712\t                    <div class=\"calibration-actions\">\n713\t                        <button class=\"calibration-btn calibration-btn-primary\" id=\"apply-suggestion-btn\" onclick=\"Proactive.applySuggestedValue('${settingKey}')\" disabled>\n714\t                            Apply Suggested Value\n715\t                        </button>\n716\t                        <button class=\"calibration-btn calibration-btn-secondary\" onclick=\"Proactive.closeCalibrationFlow()\">\n717\t                            Cancel\n718\t                        </button>\n719\t                    </div>\n720\t                </div>\n721\t            `\n722\t        };\n723\t\n724\t        content.innerHTML = steps[step] || steps.intro;\n725\t\n726\t        // Execute step-specific logic\n727\t        if (step === 'false-positive-test') {\n728\t            runCalibrationTest(settingKey, 'false-positive', 15);\n729\t        } else if (step === 'missed-motion-test') {\n730\t            runCalibrationTest(settingKey, 'missed-motion', 10);\n731\t        } else if (step === 'analyzing') {\n732\t            analyzeAndSuggest(settingKey);\n733\t        }\n734\t    }\n735\t\n736\t    /**\n737\t     * Run a calibration test with countdown timer\n738\t     */\n739\t    function runCalibrationTest(settingKey, testType, duration) {\n740\t        const timerEl = document.getElementById('calibration-timer');\n741\t        const statusEl = document.getElementById('calibration-status');\n742\t        const progressFill = document.getElementById('calibration-progress-fill');\n743\t        const startTime = Date.now();\n744\t\n745\t        // Update progress bar fill\n746\t        if (progressFill) {\n747\t            const targetWidth = testType === 'false-positive' ? '0%' : '50%';\n748\t            progressFill.style.width = targetWidth;\n749\t        }\n750\t\n751\t        // Start collecting test data\n752\t        collectTestData(settingKey, testType);\n753\t\n754\t        const interval = setInterval(() => {\n755\t            const elapsed = (Date.now() - startTime) / 1000;\n756\t            const remaining = Math.max(0, Math.ceil(duration - elapsed));\n757\t\n758\t            if (timerEl) {\n759\t                timerEl.textContent = remaining;\n760\t            }\n761\t\n762\t            // Update progress\n763\t            if (progressFill) {\n764\t                const baseWidth = testType === 'false-positive' ? 0 : 50;\n765\t                const progress = (elapsed / duration) * 50;\n766\t                progressFill.style.width = (baseWidth + progress) + '%';\n767\t            }\n768\t\n769\t            if (elapsed >= 1 && elapsed < 3) {\n770\t                if (statusEl) statusEl.textContent = 'Recording baseline...';\n771\t            } else if (elapsed >= 3 && elapsed < duration - 2) {\n772\t                if (statusEl) statusEl.textContent = testType === 'false-positive' ? 'Walking... keep moving!' : 'Holding still...';\n773\t            } else if (elapsed >= duration - 2) {\n774\t                if (statusEl) statusEl.textContent = 'Finishing up...';\n775\t            }\n776\t\n777\t            if (elapsed >= duration) {\n778\t                clearInterval(interval);\n779\t                finalizeTestData(settingKey, testType);\n780\t\n781\t                // Move to next step\n782\t                if (testType === 'false-positive') {\n783\t                    renderCalibrationStep(settingKey, 'missed-motion-test');\n784\t                } else {\n785\t                    renderCalibrationStep(settingKey, 'analyzing');\n786\t                }\n787\t            }\n788\t        }, 100);\n789\t    }\n790\t\n791\t    /**\n792\t     * Collect test data from the system\n793\t     */\n794\t    function collectTestData(settingKey, testType) {\n795\t        // Store test metadata for later analysis\n796\t        if (!window.calibrationTestData) {\n797\t            window.calibrationTestData = {};\n798\t        }\n799\t        window.calibrationTestData[testType] = {\n800\t            startTime: Date.now(),\n801\t            settingKey: settingKey\n802\t        };\n803\t\n804\t        // Notify the system to start recording for this test\n805\t        window.dispatchEvent(new CustomEvent('spaxel:calibration-start', {\n806\t            detail: { testType: testType, settingKey: settingKey }\n807\t        }));\n808\t    }\n809\t\n810\t    /**\n811\t     * Finalize test data collection\n812\t     */\n813\t    function finalizeTestData(settingKey, testType) {\n814\t        if (!window.calibrationTestData || !window.calibrationTestData[testType]) {\n815\t            return;\n816\t        }\n817\t\n818\t        window.calibrationTestData[testType].endTime = Date.now();\n819\t\n820\t        // Notify the system to stop recording\n821\t        window.dispatchEvent(new CustomEvent('spaxel:calibration-end', {\n822\t            detail: { testType: testType, settingKey: settingKey }\n823\t        }));\n824\t    }\n825\t\n826\t    /**\n827\t     * Analyze test data and suggest optimal value\n828\t     */\n829\t    function analyzeAndSuggest(settingKey) {\n830\t        // Fetch diurnal baseline status and link health data\n831\t        Promise.all([\n832\t            fetch('/api/diurnal/status').then(r => r.json()).catch(() => null),\n833\t            fetch('/api/links').then(r => r.json()).catch(() => null)\n834\t        ]).then(([diurnalData, linksData]) => {\n835\t            const suggestion = calculateSuggestedValue(settingKey, diurnalData, linksData);\n836\t            renderSuggestion(settingKey, suggestion);\n837\t        }).catch(err => {\n838\t            console.error('Failed to fetch calibration data:', err);\n839\t            // Show fallback suggestion\n840\t            renderSuggestion(settingKey, getFallbackSuggestion(settingKey));\n841\t        });\n842\t    }\n843\t\n844\t    /**\n845\t     * Calculate suggested value based on system data\n846\t     */\n847\t    function calculateSuggestedValue(settingKey, diurnalData, linksData) {\n848\t        const suggestion = {\n849\t            value: null,\n850\t            reason: '',\n851\t            metrics: []\n852\t        };\n853\t\n854\t        const now = new Date();\n855\t        const currentHour = now.getHours();\n856\t\n857\t        // Get average health score across all links (higher is better, 0-1 range)\n858\t        let avgHealthScore = 0.5; // default fallback\n859\t        let activeLinkCount = 0;\n860\t\n861\t        if (Array.isArray(linksData)) {\n862\t            const healthScores = linksData.map(l => l.health_score || 0.5).filter(s => s >= 0);\n863\t            if (healthScores.length > 0) {\n864\t                avgHealthScore = healthScores.reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0) / healthScores.length;\n865\t                activeLinkCount = linksData.length;\n866\t            }\n867\t        }\n868\t\n869\t        // Get diurnal baseline readiness/learning status\n870\t        let diurnalReady = false;\n871\t        let learningProgress = 0;\n872\t\n873\t        if (Array.isArray(diurnalData) && diurnalData.length > 0) {\n874\t            // diurnalData is an array of DiurnalLearningStatus objects\n875\t            const readyCount = diurnalData.filter(d => d.is_ready).length;\n876\t            diurnalReady = readyCount > (diurnalData.length / 2); // Majority ready\n877\t\n878\t            // Average learning progress (backend returns 'progress' field, 0-100 range)\n879\t            const progressValues = diurnalData.map(d => (d.progress || 0) / 100).filter(p => p >= 0);\n880\t            if (progressValues.length > 0) {\n881\t                learningProgress = progressValues.reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0) / progressValues.length;\n882\t            }\n883\t        }\n884\t\n885\t        // Calculate suggestion based on setting type\n886\t        // Note: avgHealthScore is 0-1 where higher is better (unlike raw SNR)\n887\t        switch (settingKey) {\n888\t            case 'delta_rms_threshold':\n889\t                // Lower threshold for high health scores, higher for low health scores\n890\t                // Range: 0.01 - 0.10\n891\t                if (avgHealthScore > 0.8) {\n892\t                    suggestion.value = 0.02;\n893\t                    suggestion.reason = 'Your space has excellent link health. A lower threshold will detect subtle movements while minimizing false positives.';\n894\t                } else if (avgHealthScore > 0.6) {\n895\t                    suggestion.value = 0.03;\n896\t                    suggestion.reason = 'Your space has good link health. This threshold balances sensitivity with noise immunity.';\n897\t                } else {\n898\t                    suggestion.value = 0.05;\n899\t                    suggestion.reason = 'Your space has lower link health. A higher threshold reduces false positives from environmental noise.';\n900\t                }\n901\t                // Adjust based on diurnal readiness\n902\t                if (diurnalReady && learningProgress < 0.5) {\n903\t                    suggestion.value *= 1.3; // Still learning needs higher threshold\n904\t                    suggestion.reason += ' Adjusted up since your baselines are still learning.';\n905\t                }\n906\t                break;\n907\t\n908\t            case 'breathing_sensitivity':\n909\t                // Range: 0.001 - 0.02\n910\t                if (avgHealthScore > 0.75) {\n911\t                    suggestion.value = 0.005;\n912\t                    suggestion.reason = 'High link health enables fine-grained breathing detection.';\n913\t                } else if (avgHealthScore > 0.55) {\n914\t                    suggestion.value = 0.008;\n915\t                    suggestion.reason = 'Good link health for reliable breathing detection.';\n916\t                } else {\n917\t                    suggestion.value = 0.015;\n918\t                    suggestion.reason = 'Lower link health requires higher sensitivity for breathing detection.';\n919\t                }\n920\t                break;\n921\t\n922\t            case 'tau_s':\n923\t                // Baseline time constant: 5 - 120 seconds\n924\t                if (diurnalReady && learningProgress > 0.8) {\n925\t                    suggestion.value = 30;\n926\t                    suggestion.reason = 'Your diurnal baselines are well-calibrated. A 30-second time constant adapts quickly to real changes.';\n927\t                } else if (diurnalReady || learningProgress > 0.5) {\n928\t                    suggestion.value = 60;\n929\t                    suggestion.reason = 'Moderate baseline stability. A 60-second time constant provides stable adaptation.';\n930\t                } else {\n931\t                    suggestion.value = 120;\n932\t                    suggestion.reason = 'Your environment is still learning baselines. A longer time constant (120s) provides more stable detection.';\n933\t                }\n934\t                break;\n935\t\n936\t            case 'fresnel_decay':\n937\t                // Zone decay rate: 1.0 - 4.0\n938\t                if (avgHealthScore > 0.75) {\n939\t                    suggestion.value = 2.5;\n940\t                    suggestion.reason = 'Strong link health supports tighter zone focus for better localization accuracy.';\n941\t                } else if (avgHealthScore > 0.55) {\n942\t                    suggestion.value = 2.0;\n943\t                    suggestion.reason = 'Balanced decay rate for your link health.';\n944\t                } else {\n945\t                    suggestion.value = 1.5;\n946\t                    suggestion.reason = 'Lower link health benefits from broader zone contribution.';\n947\t                }\n948\t                break;\n949\t\n950\t            case 'n_subcarriers':\n951\t                // Subcarrier count: 8 - 16\n952\t                if (avgHealthScore > 0.75) {\n953\t                    suggestion.value = 16;\n954\t                    suggestion.reason = 'Excellent link health supports using all 16 subcarriers for maximum detail.';\n955\t                } else if (avgHealthScore > 0.55) {\n956\t                    suggestion.value = 12;\n957\t                    suggestion.reason = 'Good link health. 12 subcarriers balance detail with noise immunity.';\n958\t                } else {\n959\t                    suggestion.value = 8;\n960\t                    suggestion.reason = 'Lower link health. Fewer subcarriers reduce noise impact.';\n961\t                }\n962\t                break;\n963\t\n964\t            default:\n965\t                suggestion.value = 0.03;\n966\t                suggestion.reason = 'Default suggestion based on average system performance.';\n967\t        }\n968\t\n969\t        // Build metrics display\n970\t        const healthPercent = Math.round(avgHealthScore * 100);\n971\t        suggestion.metrics = [\n972\t            { label: 'Link Health', value: healthPercent + '%' },\n973\t            { label: 'Diurnal Ready', value: diurnalReady ? 'Yes' : 'Learning' },\n974\t            { label: 'Active Links', value: activeLinkCount.toString() }\n975\t        ];\n976\t\n977\t        return suggestion;\n978\t    }\n979\t\n980\t    /**\n981\t     * Get fallback suggestion when API data is unavailable\n982\t     */\n983\t    function getFallbackSuggestion(settingKey) {\n984\t        const defaults = {\n985\t            'delta_rms_threshold': { value: 0.03, reason: 'Default value for typical home environments.' },\n986\t            'breathing_sensitivity': { value: 0.008, reason: 'Default sensitivity for reliable breathing detection.' },\n987\t            'tau_s': { value: 60, reason: 'Default 60-second time constant for stable adaptation.' },\n988\t            'fresnel_decay': { value: 2.0, reason: 'Default inverse-square decay for balanced localization.' },\n989\t            'n_subcarriers': { value: 12, reason: 'Default 12 subcarriers for balanced performance.' }\n990\t        };\n991\t        return defaults[settingKey] || { value: 0.03, reason: 'Default value.' };\n992\t    }\n993\t\n994\t    /**\n995\t     * Render the suggestion step with calculated values\n996\t     */\n997\t    function </div>\n1014\t                <div class=\"calibration-metrics\">\n1015\t                    <h4>Based on your space:</h4>\n1016\t                    ${suggestion.metrics.map(m => `\n1017\t                        <div class=\"calibration-metric\">\n1018\t                            <span class=\"metric-label\">${m.label}:</span>\n1019\t                            <span onclick=\"Proactive.closeCalibrationFlow()\">\n1028\t                        Cancel\n1029\t                    </button>\n1030\t                </div>\n1031\t            </div>\n1032\t        `;\n1033\t    }\n1034\t\n1035\t    /**\n1036\t     * Format a suggested value for display\n1037\t     */\n1038\t    function formatSuggestedValue(settingKey, value) {\n1039\t        if (settingKey === 'tau_s') {\n1040\t            return value + ' seconds';\n1041\t        } else if (settingKey === 'n_subcarriers') {\n1042\t            return value + ' subcarriers';\n1043\t        } else if (settingKey === 'fresnel_decay') {\n1044\t            return value.toFixed(1);\n1045\t        }\n1046\t        return value.toFixed(3);\n1047\t    }\n1048\t\n1049\t    /**\n1050\t     * Apply the suggested value to the setting\n1051\t     */\n1052\t    function applySuggestedValue(settingKey, value) {\n1053\t        // Show loading state\n1054\t        const applyBtn = }\n1059\t\n1060\t        // Build settings payload\n1061\t        const settings = {};\n1062\t        settings[settingKey] = value;\n1063\t\n1064\t        // Send to API\n1065\t err);\n1084\t            showCalibrationError();\n1085\t        });\n1086\t    }\n1087\t\n1088\t    /**\n1089\t     * Show calibration success message\n1090\t     */\n1091\t    function `;\n1131\t    }\n1132\t\n1133\t    /**\n1134\t     * Close the calibration flow modal\n1135\t     */\n1136\t    function closeCalibrationFlow() {\n1137\t        const modal = }\n1147\t\n1148\t    /**\n1149\t     * Save setting change history to localStorage\n1150\t     */\n1151\t    function saveSettingHistory() {\n1152\t        try {\n1153\t }\n1157\t    }\n1158\t\n1159\t    /**\n1160\t     * Save setting hint shown timestamps\n1161\t     */\n1162\t    function saveSettingHintShown() {\n1163\t        try {\n1164\t            localStorage.setItem('spaxel_setting_hints_shown', JSON.stringify(settingChangeHintShown));\n1165\t        } catch (e) {\n1166\t            console.warn('Failed to save hint shown state:', e);\n1167\t        }\n1168\t    }\n1169\t\n1170\t    /**\n1171\t     * Format a setting key for display\n1172\t     */\n1173\t    function formatSettingName(key) {\n1174\t        const names = {\n1175\t            'delta_rms_threshold': 'Motion Threshold',\n1176\t            'breathing_sensitivity': 'Breathing Sensitivity',\n1177\t            'tau_s': 'Baseline Time Constant',\n1178\t            'fresnel_decay': 'Fresnel Weight Decay',\n1179\t            'n_subcarriers': 'Subcarrier Count'\n1180\t        };\n1181\t        return names[key] || key;\n1182\t    }\n1183\t\n1184\t    // ===== Post-Feedback Explanations =====\n1185\t\n1186\t    /**\n1187\t     * Show explanation after false positive feedback\n1188\t     */\n1189\t    function showFeedbackExplanation(eventData) {\n1190\t        if (!eventData || !eventData.explainability) {\n1191\t            return;\n1192\t        }\n1193\t\n1194\t        const explanation = eventData.explainability;\n1195\t        const contributingLinks = explanation.contributing_links || [];\n1196\t        const diagnosis = explanation.diagnosis || null;\n1197\t\n1198\t        // Find the primary contributing link\n1199\t        const primaryLink = contributingLinks.length > 0 ? contributingLinks[0] : null;\n1200\t\n1201\t        let explanationText = '';\n1202\t\n1203\t        if (primaryLink) {\n1204\t            const linkName = formatLinkID(primaryLink.link_id);\n1205\t            const deltaRMS = primaryLink.delta_rms?.toFixed(4) || 'N/A';\n1206\t            const threshold = 0.02; // Standard threshold\n1207\t            const ratio = (primaryLink.delta_rms / threshold).toFixed(1);\n1208\t\n1209\t            explanationText = `The system detected motion here because: <strong>${linkName}</strong>'s signal (deltaRMS: ${deltaRMS}) exceeded the motion threshold by <strong>${ratio}x</strong>.`;\n1210\t\n1211\t            // Add root cause from diagnostic if available\n1212\t            if (diagnosis) {\n1213\t                explanationText += `<br><br><strong>Possible cause:</strong> ${diagnosis.detail}`;\n1214\t\n1215\t                if (diagnosis.advice) {\n1216\t                    explanationText += `<br><strong>What to do:</strong> ${diagnosis.advice}`;\n1217\t                }\n1218\t                explanationText += `<br><br><em>We've noted this and will apply corrections.</em>`;\n1219\t            } else {\n1220\t                explanationText += `<br><br><strong>Possible cause:</strong> Ambient RF interference or environmental changes. We've noted this and will apply corrections.`;\n1221\t            }\n1222\t        } else {\n1223\t            explanationText = 'The system detected motion based on signal patterns across multiple links. We\\'ve noted this feedback to improve accuracy.';\n1224\t        }\n1225\t\n1226\t        // Create explanation element\n1227\t        const explanationDiv = document.createElement('div');\n1228\t        explanationDiv.className = 'feedback-explanation';\n1229\t        explanationDiv.innerHTML = `\n1230\t            <div class=\"explanation-header\">\n1231\t                <span class=\"explanation-title\">Why did this happen?</span>\n1232\t            </div>\n1233\t            <div class=\"explanation-content\">\n1234\t                <p>${explanationText}</p>\n1235\t                ${contributingLinks.length > 1 ? `<p class=\"explanation-additional-links\">Contributing links: ${contributingLinks.map(l => formatLinkID(l.link_id)).join(', ')}</p>` : ''}\n1236\t            </div>\n1237\t        `;\n1238\t\n1239\t        return explanationDiv;\n1240\t    }\n1241\t\n1242\t    /**\n1243\t     * Fetch diagnostic info for a link at a specific time\n1244\t     */\n1245\t    function fetchDiagnosticForLink(linkID, timestamp) {\n1246\t        // Using the correct endpoint: /api/diagnostics/link/{linkID}?timestamp={ms}\n1247\t        return fetch(`/api/diagnostics/link/${encodeURIComponent(linkID)}?timestamp=${timestamp}`)\n1248\t            .then(res => {\n1249\t                if (!res.ok) {\n1250\t                    throw new Error(`HTTP ${res.status}: ${res.statusText}`);\n1251\t                }\n1252\t                return res.json();\n1253\t            })\n1254\t            .catch(err => {\n1255\t                console.error('Failed to fetch diagnostic:', err);\n1256\t                return null;\n1257\t            });\n1258\t    }\n1259\t\n1260\t    // ===== Helpers =====\n1261\t\n1262\t    function formatLinkID(linkID) {\n1263\t        if (!linkID) {\n1264\t            return 'Unknown Link';\n1265\t        }\n1266\t        // Format MAC address pairs nicely\n1267\t        const parts = linkID.split(':');\n1268\t        if (parts.length === 2) {\n1269\t            const mac1 = parts[0].substring(0, 8); // First 8 chars of first MAC\n1270\t            const mac2 = parts[1].substring(0, 8); // First 8 chars of second MAC\n1271\t            return `${mac1} → ${mac2}`;\n1272\t        }\n1273\t        return linkID.substring(0, 16) + '...';\n1274\t    }\n1275\t\n1276\t    // ===== Public API =====\n1277\t    window.Proactive = {\n1278\t        // Quality monitoring\n1279\t        monitorLinkQuality: monitorLinkQuality,\n1280\t        dismissQualityPrompt: dismissQualityPrompt,\n1281\t        dismissQualityPromptForToday: dismissQualityPromptForToday,\n1282\t        diagnoseLink: diagnoseLink,\n1283\t\n1284\t        // Setting fetchDiagnosticForLink,\n1297\t\n1298\t        // Initialization\n1299\t        init: function() {\n1300\t            loadDismissedPrompts();\n1301\t\n1302\t            // Listen for WebSocket window.addEventListener('spaxel:feedback', (e) => {\n1311\t                if (e.detail && e.detail.type === 'incorrect') {\n1312\t                    const explanation = feedbackPanel.querySelector('.feedback-content');\n1318\t                            if (contentArea) {\n1319\t                                contentArea.appendChild(explanation);\n1320\t                            }\n1321\t                        }\n1322\t                    }\n1323\t                }\n1324\t            });\n1325\t\n1326\t            // Check for server-side repeated edit hint flag\n1327\t            checkServerEditHint();\n1328\t        }\n1329\t    };\n1330\t\n1331\t    /**\n1332\t     * Check for server-side repeated edit hint flag\n1333\t     */\n1334\t    function {\n1339\t                    // Show the hint - the server detected repeated edits\n1340\t                    showSettingChangeHint('detected_by_server');\n1341\t                }\n1342\t            })\n1343\t            .catch(err => {\n1344\t                // Ignore errors - this is a nice-to-have feature\n1345\t            });\n1346\t    }\n1347\t\n1348\t    // Initialize on load\n1349\t PULSE_CYCLE;\n293\t\n294\t            // Opacity oscillates: 0.3 -> 0.8 -> 0.3\n295\t            const intensity = 0.3 + 0.5 * (1 - Math.abs(phase - 0.5) * 2);\n296\t\n297\t            // Apply Detection =====\n468\t\n469\t    /**\n470\t     * Track a settings change for repeated-change detection\n471\t     */\n472\t    function trackSettingChange(settingKey, settingValue) {\n473\t        if (!QUALIFYING_SETTINGS.has(settingKey)) {\n474\t            return; // Not a qualifying setting\n475\t        }\n476\t\n477\t        const now = Date.now();\n478\t        const windowMs = 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000; // 24 hours\n479\t\n480\t        // Initialize history for this setting if needed\n481\t        if (!settingChangeHistory[settingKey]) {\n482\t            settingChangeHistory[settingKey] = [];\n483\t        }\n484\t\n485\t        // Add new change\n486\t        settingChangeHistory[settingKey].push({\n487\t            timestamp: now,\n488\t            value: settingValue\n489\t        });\n490\t\n491\t        // Remove old changes outside the 24h window\n492\t        const cutoff = now - windowMs;\n493\t        settingChangeHistory[settingKey] = settingChangeHistory[settingKey].filter(\n494\t            change => change.timestamp > cutoff\n495\t        );\n496\t\n497\t        // Save to localStorage\n498\t        saveSettingHistory();\n499\t\n500\t        // Check if we should show a hint\n501\t        checkSettingChangeHint(settingKey);\n502\t    }\n503\t\n504\t    /**\n505\t     * Check if a setting change (settingChangeHintShown[settingKey]) {\n510\t            const lastShown = settingChangeHintShown[settingKey];\n511\t            const cooldownMs = 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000; // 24 hour cooldown\n512\t            if (Date.now() - lastShown < cooldownMs) {\n513\t                return; // Still in cooldown\n514\t            }\n515\t        }\n516\t\n517\t        const changes = settingChangeHistory[settingKey] || [];\n518\t        if (changes.length >= 3) {\n519\t            // Show the hint\n520\t            showSettingChangeHint(settingKey);\n521\t            settingChangeHintShown[settingKey] = Date.now();\n522\t            saveSettingHintShown();\n523\t        }\n524\t    }\n525\t\n526\t    /**\n527\t     * Show a hint for repeated setting changes\n528\t     */\n529\t    function showSettingChangeHint(settingKey) {\n530\t        const settingName = formatSettingName(settingKey);\n531\t\n532\t        // Remove existing hint if present\n533\t        const existing = document.getElementById('setting-change-hint');\n534\t        if (existing) {\n535\t            existing.remove();\n536\t        }\n537\t\n538\t        const hint = `;\n559\t\n560\t        document.body.appendChild(hint);\n561\t    }\n562\t\n563\t    /**\n564\t     * Dismiss the setting change hint\n565\t     */\n566\t    function dismissSettingHint() {\n567\t        const hint = document.getElementById('setting-change-hint');\n568\t        if (hint) {\n569\t            hint.remove();\n570\t        }\n571\t    }\n572\t\n573\t    /**\n574\t     * Start the </div>\n606\t                <div class=\"calibration-flow-content\" id=\"calibration-flow-content\">\n607\t                    <!-- Steps will be rendered here -->\n608\t                </div>\n609\t            </div>\n610\t        `;\n611\t\n612\t        document.body.appendChild(modal);\n613\t\n614\t        // Start with the introduction step\n615\t        renderCalibrationStep(settingKey,                <p>I'll guide you through two quick tests to analyze your space and suggest the best ${formatSettingName(settingKey)} value.</p>\n631\t                    <div       <span class=\"overview-text\">Walk around your room to test for false positives</span>\n635\t                        </div>\n636\t                        <div class=\"overview-step\">\n637\t                            <span class=\"overview-number\">2</span>\n638\t                            <span class=\"overview-text\">Sit still to test for missed motion detection</span>\n639\t                        </div>\n640\t                        <div class=\"overview-step\">\n641\t                            <span class=\"overview-number\">3</span>\n642\t                            <span        </button>\n648\t                </div>\n649\t            `,\n650\t\n651\t            'false-positive-test': `\n652\t                <div class=\"calibration-step                 <h3>Analyzing your space...</h3>\n692\t                    <p>Collecting diurnal baseline data and link health metrics to calculate the optimal value.</p>\n693\t                </div>\n694\t            `,\n695\t\n696\t            suggestion: `\n697\t                <div class=\"calibration-step\">\n698\t                    <div class=\"calibration-icon\">✨</div>\n699\t                    <h3>Here's my recommendation</h3>\n700\t                    <div class=\"calibration-suggestion\">\n701\t                        <div class=\"suggestion-value\">\n702\t                            <span class=\"suggestion-label\">Suggested ${formatSettingName(settingKey)}:</span>\n703\t                            <span class=\"suggestion-number\" id=\"suggested-value\">--</span>\n704\t                        </div>\n705\t                        <div class=\"suggestion-reason\" id=\"suggestion-reason\">\n706\t                            Calculating...\n707\t                        </div>\n708\t                    </div>\n709\t                    <div class=\"calibration-metrics\" id=\"calibration-metrics\">\n710\t                        <!-- Metrics will be populated -->\n711\t                    </div>\n712\t                    <div class=\"calibration-actions\">\n713\t                        <button class=\"calibration-btn calibration-btn-primary\"                       <button class=\"calibration-btn calibration-btn-secondary\" onclick=\"Proactive.closeCalibrationFlow()\">\n717\t                            Cancel\n718\t                        </button>\n719\t                    </div>\n720\t                </div>\n721\t            `\n722\t        };\n723\t\n724\t        content.innerHTML = steps[step] || steps.intro;\n725\t\n726\t        // Execute step-specific logic\n727\t        if (step === 'false-positive-test') {\n728\t            runCalibrationTest(settingKey, 'false-positive', 15);\n729\t        } else if (step === 'missed-motion-test') {\n730\t            runCalibrationTest(settingKey, 'missed-motion', 10);\n731\t        } else if (step === 'analyzing') {\n732\t            analyzeAndSuggest(settingKey);\n733\t        }\n734\t    }\n735\t\n736\t    /**\n737\t     * Run a calibration test with countdown timer\n738\t     */\n739\t    function runCalibrationTest(settingKey, testType, duration) {\n740\t        const timerEl = document.getElementById('calibration-timer');\n741\t        const statusEl = document.getElementById('calibration-status');\n742\t        const progressFill = document.getElementById('calibration-progress-fill');\n743\t        const startTime = Date.now();\n744\t\n745\t        // Update progress bar fill\n746\t        if (progressFill) {\n747\t            const targetWidth = testType === 'false-positive' ? '0%' : '50%';\n748\t            progressFill.style.width = targetWidth;\n749\t        }\n750\t\n751\t        // Start collecting test data\n752\t        collectTestData(settingKey, testType);\n753\t\n754\t        const interval = setInterval(() => {\n755\t            const elapsed = (Date.now() - startTime) / 1000;\n756\t            const remaining = Math.max(0, Math.ceil(duration - elapsed));\n757\t\n758\t            if (timerEl) {\n759\t                timerEl.textContent = remaining;\n760\t            }\n761\t\n762\t            // Update progress\n763\t            if (progressFill) {\n764\t                const baseWidth = testType === 'false-positive' ? 0 : 50;\n765\t                const progress = (elapsed / duration) * 50;\n766\t                progressFill.style.width = (baseWidth + progress) + '%';\n767\t            }\n768\t\n769\t            if (elapsed >= 1 && elapsed < 3) {\n770\t                if (statusEl) statusEl.textContent = 'Recording baseline...';\n771\t            } else if (elapsed >= 3 && elapsed < duration - 2) {\n772\t                if (statusEl) statusEl.textContent = testType === 'false-positive' ? 'Walking... keep moving!' : 'Holding still...';\n773\t            } else if (elapsed >= duration - 2) {\n774\t                if (statusEl) statusEl.textContent = 'Finishing up...';\n775\t            }\n776\t\n777\t            if (elapsed >= duration) {\n778\t                clearInterval(interval);\n779\t                finalizeTestData(settingKey, testType);\n780\t\n781\t                // Move to next step\n782\t                if (testType === 'false-positive') {\n783\t                    renderCalibrationStep(settingKey, 'missed-motion-test');\n784\t                } else {\n785\t                    renderCalibrationStep(settingKey, 'analyzing');\n786\t                }\n787\t            }\n788\t        }, 100);\n789\t    }\n790\t\n791\t    /**\n792\t     * Collect test data from the system\n793\t     */\n794\t    function collectTestData(settingKey, testType) {\n795\t        // Store test metadata for later analysis\n796\t        if (!window.calibrationTestData) {\n797\t            window.calibrationTestData = {};\n798\t        }\n799\t        window.calibrationTestData[testType] = {\n800\t            startTime: Date.now(),\n801\t            settingKey: settingKey\n802\t        };\n803\t\n804\t        // Notify the system to start recording for this test\n805\t        window.dispatchEvent(new CustomEvent('spaxel:calibration-start', {\n806\t            detail: { testType: testType, settingKey: settingKey }\n807\t        }));\n808\t    }\n809\t\n810\t    /**\n811\t     * Finalize test data collection\n812\t     */\n813\t    function finalizeTestData(settingKey, testType) {\n814\t        if (!window.calibrationTestData || !window.calibrationTestData[testType]) {\n815\t            return;\n816\t        }\n817\t\n818\t        window.calibrationTestData[testType].endTime = Date.now();\n819\t\n820\t        // Notify the system to stop recording\n821\t        window.dispatchEvent(new CustomEvent('spaxel:calibration-end', {\n822\t            detail: { testType: testType, settingKey: settingKey }\n823\t        }));\n824\t    }\n825\t\n826\t    /**\n827\t     * Analyze test data and suggest optimal value\n828\t     */\n829\t    function analyzeAndSuggest(settingKey) {\n830\t        // Fetch diurnal baseline status and link health data\n831\t        Promise.all([\n832\t            fetch('/api/diurnal/status').then(r => r.json()).catch(() => null),\n833\t            fetch('/api/links').then(r => r.json()).catch(() => null)\n834\t        ]).then(([diurnalData, linksData]) => {\n835\t            const suggestion = calculateSuggestedValue(settingKey, diurnalData, linksData);\n836\t            renderSuggestion(settingKey, suggestion);\n837\t        }).catch(err => {\n838\t            console.error('Failed to fetch calibration data:', err);\n839\t            // Show fallback suggestion\n840\t            renderSuggestion(settingKey, getFallbackSuggestion(settingKey));\n841\t        });\n842\t    }\n843\t\n844\t    /**\n845\t     * Calculate suggested value based on system data\n846\t     */\n847\t    function calculateSuggestedValue(settingKey, diurnalData, linksData) {\n848\t        const suggestion = {\n849\t            value: null,\n850\t            reason: '',\n851\t            metrics: []\n852\t        };\n853\t\n854\t        const now = new Date();\n855\t        const currentHour = now.getHours();\n856\t\n857\t        // Get average health score across all links (higher is better, 0-1 range)\n858\t        let avgHealthScore = 0.5; // default fallback\n859\t        let activeLinkCount = 0;\n860\t\n861\t        if (Array.isArray(linksData)) {\n862\t            const healthScores = linksData.map(l => l.health_score || 0.5).filter(s => s >= 0);\n863\t            if (healthScores.length > 0) {\n864\t                avgHealthScore = healthScores.reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0) / healthScores.length;\n865\t                activeLinkCount = linksData.length;\n866\t            }\n867\t        }\n868\t\n869\t        // Get diurnal baseline readiness/learning status\n870\t        let diurnalReady = false;\n871\t        let learningProgress = 0;\n872\t\n873\t        if (Array.isArray(diurnalData) && diurnalData.length > 0) {\n874\t            // diurnalData is an array of DiurnalLearningStatus objects\n875\t            const readyCount = diurnalData.filter(d => d.is_ready).length;\n876\t            diurnalReady = readyCount > (diurnalData.length / 2); // Majority ready\n877\t\n878\t            // Average learning progress (backend returns 'progress' field, 0-100 range)\n879\t            const progressValues = diurnalData.map(d => (d.progress || 0) / 100).filter(p => p >= 0);\n880\t            if (progressValues.length > 0) {\n881\t                learningProgress = progressValues.reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0) / progressValues.length;\n882\t            }\n883\t        }\n884\t\n885\t        // Calculate suggestion based on setting type\n886\t        // Note: avgHealthScore is 0-1 where higher is better (unlike raw SNR)\n887\t        switch (settingKey) {\n888\t            case 'delta_rms_threshold':\n889\t                // Lower threshold for high health scores, higher for low health scores\n890\t                // Range: 0.01 - 0.10\n891\t                if (avgHealthScore > 0.8) {\n892\t                    suggestion.value = 0.02;\n893\t                    suggestion.reason = 'Your space has excellent link health. A lower threshold will detect subtle movements while minimizing false positives.';\n894\t                } else if (avgHealthScore > 0.6) {\n895\t                    suggestion.value = 0.03;\n896\t                    suggestion.reason = 'Your space has good link health. This threshold balances sensitivity with noise immunity.';\n897\t                } else {\n898\t                    suggestion.value = 0.05;\n899\t                    suggestion.reason = 'Your space has lower link health. A higher threshold reduces false positives from environmental noise.';\n900\t                }\n901\t                // Adjust based on diurnal readiness\n902\t                if (diurnalReady && learningProgress < 0.5) {\n903\t                    suggestion.value *= 1.3; // Still learning needs higher threshold\n904\t                    suggestion.reason += ' Adjusted up since your baselines are still learning.';\n905\t                }\n906\t                break;\n907\t\n908\t            case 'breathing_sensitivity':\n909\t                // Range: 0.001 - 0.02\n910\t                if (avgHealthScore > 0.75) {\n911\t                    suggestion.value = 0.005;\n912\t                    suggestion.reason = 'High link health enables fine-grained breathing detection.';\n913\t                } else if (avgHealthScore > 0.55) {\n914\t                    suggestion.value = 0.008;\n915\t                    suggestion.reason = 'Good link health for reliable breathing detection.';\n916\t                } else {\n917\t                    suggestion.value = 0.015;\n918\t                    suggestion.reason = 'Lower link health requires higher sensitivity for breathing detection.';\n919\t                }\n920\t                break;\n921\t\n922\t            case 'tau_s':\n923\t                // Baseline time constant: 5 - 120 seconds\n924\t                if (diurnalReady && learningProgress > 0.8) {\n925\t                    suggestion.value = 30;\n926\t                    suggestion.reason = 'Your diurnal baselines are well-calibrated. A 30-second time constant adapts quickly to real changes.';\n927\t                } else if (diurnalReady || learningProgress > 0.5) {\n928\t                    suggestion.value = 60;\n929\t                    suggestion.reason = 'Moderate baseline stability. A 60-second time constant provides stable adaptation.';\n930\t                } else {\n931\t                    suggestion.value = 120;\n932\t                    suggestion.reason = 'Your environment is still learning baselines. A longer time constant (120s) provides more stable detection.';\n933\t                }\n934\t                break;\n935\t\n936\t            case 'fresnel_decay':\n937\t                // Zone decay rate: 1.0 - 4.0\n938\t                if (avgHealthScore > 0.75) {\n939\t                    suggestion.value = 2.5;\n940\t                    suggestion.reason = 'Strong link health supports tighter zone focus for better localization accuracy.';\n941\t                } else if (avgHealthScore > 0.55) {\n942\t                    suggestion.value = 2.0;\n943\t                    suggestion.reason = 'Balanced decay rate for your link health.';\n944\t                } else {\n945\t                    suggestion.value = 1.5;\n946\t                    suggestion.reason = 'Lower link health benefits from broader zone contribution.';\n947\t                }\n948\t                break;\n949\t\n950\t            case 'n_subcarriers':\n951\t                // Subcarrier count: 8 - 16\n952\t                if (avgHealthScore > 0.75) {\n953\t                    suggestion.value = 16;\n954\t                    suggestion.reason = 'Excellent link health supports using all 16 subcarriers for maximum detail.';\n955\t                } else if (avgHealthScore > 0.55) {\n956\t                    suggestion.value = 12;\n957\t                    suggestion.reason = 'Good link health. 12 subcarriers balance detail with noise immunity.';\n958\t                } else {\n959\t                    suggestion.value = 8;\n960\t                    suggestion.reason = 'Lower link health. Fewer subcarriers reduce noise impact.';\n961\t                }\n962\t                break;\n963\t\n964\t            default:\n965\t                suggestion.value = 0.03;\n966\t                suggestion.reason = 'Default suggestion based on average system performance.';\n967\t        }\n968\t\n969\t        // Build metrics display\n970\t        const healthPercent = Math.round(avgHealthScore * 100);\n971\t        suggestion.metrics = [\n972\t            { label: 'Link Health', value: healthPercent + '%' },\n973\t            { label: 'Diurnal Ready', value: diurnalReady ? 'Yes' : 'Learning' },\n974\t            { label: 'Active Links', value: activeLinkCount.toString() }\n975\t        ];\n976\t\n977\t        return suggestion;\n978\t    }\n979\t\n980\t    /**\n981\t     * Get fallback suggestion when API data is unavailable\n982\t     */\n983\t    function getFallbackSuggestion(settingKey) {\n984\t        const defaults = {\n985\t            'delta_rms_threshold': { value: 0.03, reason: 'Default value for typical home environments.' },\n986\t            'breathing_sensitivity': { value: 0.008, reason: 'Default sensitivity for reliable breathing detection.' },\n987\t            'tau_s': { value: 60, reason: 'Default 60-second time constant for stable adaptation.' },\n988\t            'fresnel_decay': { value: 2.0, reason: 'Default inverse-square decay for balanced localization.' },\n989\t            'n_subcarriers': { value: 12, reason: 'Default 12 subcarriers for balanced performance.' }\n990\t        };\n991\t        return defaults[settingKey] || { value: 0.03, reason: 'Default value.' };\n992\t    }\n993\t\n994\t    /**\n995\t     * Render the suggestion step with calculated values\n996\t     */\n997\t    function renderSuggestion(settingKey, suggestion) {\n998\t        const content = document.getElementById('calibration-flow-content');\n999\t        if (!content) return;\n1000\t\n1001\t        const formattedValue = formatSuggestedValue(settingKey, suggestion.value);\n1002\t\n1003\t        content.innerHTML = `\n1004\t            <div class=\"calibration-step\">\n1005\t                <div class=\"calibration-icon\">✨</div>\n1006\t                <h3>Here's my recommendation</h3>\n1007\t                <div class=\"calibration-suggestion\">\n1008\t                    <div class=\"suggestion-value\">\n1009\t                        <span class=\"suggestion-label\">Suggested ${formatSettingName(settingKey)}:</span>\n1010\t                        <span class=\"suggestion-number\">${formattedValue}</span>\n1011\t                    </div>\n1012\t                    <div class=\"suggestion-reason\">${suggestion.reason}</div>\n1013\t                </div>\n1014\t                <div class=\"calibration-metrics\">\n1015\t                    <h4>Based on your space:</h4>\n1016\t                    ${suggestion.metrics.map(m => `\n1017\t                        <div class=\"calibration-metric\">\n1018\t                            <span class=\"metric-label\">${m.label}:</span>\n1019\t                            <span class=\"metric-value\">${m.value}</span>\n1020\t                        </div>\n1021\t                    `).join('')}\n1022\t                </div>\n1023\t                <div class=\"calibration-actions\">\n1024\t                    <button class=\"calibration-btn calibration-btn-primary\" onclick=\"Proactive.applySuggestedValue('${settingKey}', ${suggestion.value})\">\n1025\t                        Apply Suggested Value\n1026\t                    </button>\n1027\t                    <button class=\"calibration-btn calibration-btn-secondary\" onclick=\"Proactive.closeCalibrationFlow()\">\n1028\t                        Cancel\n1029\t                    </button>\n1030\t                </div>\n1031\t            </div>\n1032\t        `;\n1033\t    }\n1034\t\n1035\t    /**\n1036\t     * Format a suggested value for display\n1037\t     */\n1038\t    function formatSuggestedValue(settingKey, value) {\n1039\t        if (settingKey === 'tau_s') {\n1040\t            return value + ' seconds';\n1041\t        } else if (settingKey === 'n_subcarriers') {\n1042\t            return value + ' subcarriers';\n1043\t        } else if (settingKey === 'fresnel_decay') {\n1044\t            return value.toFixed(1);\n1045\t        }\n1046\t        return value.toFixed(3);\n1047\t    }\n1048\t\n1049\t    /**\n1050\t     * Apply the suggested value to the setting\n1051\t     */\n1052\t    function applySuggestedValue(settingKey, value) {\n1053\t        // Show loading state\n1054\t        const applyBtn = document.querySelector('.calibration-btn-primary');\n1055\t        if (applyBtn) {\n1056\t            applyBtn.disabled = true;\n1057\t            applyBtn.textContent = 'Applying...';\n1058\t        }\n1059\t\n1060\t        // Build settings payload\n1061\t        const settings = {};\n1062\t        settings[settingKey] = value;\n1063\t\n1064\t        // Send to API\n1065\t        fetch('/api/settings', {\n1066\t            method: 'PATCH',\n1067\t            headers: {\n1068\t                'Content-Type': 'application/json'\n1069\t            },\n1070\t            body: JSON.stringify(settings)\n1071\t        })\n1072\t        .then(res => res.json())\n1073\t        .then(data => {\n1074\t            // Show success message\n1075\t }\n1147\t\n1148\t    /**\n1149\t     * Save setting change history to localStorage\n1150\t     */\n1151\t    function saveSettingHistory() {\n1152\t        try {\n1153\t        }\n1168\t    }\n1169\t\n1170\t    /**\n1171\t     * Format a setting key for display\n1172\t     */\n1173\t    function formatSettingName(key) {\n1174\t        const names = {\n1175\t            'delta_rms_threshold': 'Motion Threshold',\n1176\t            'breathing_sensitivity': 'Breathing Sensitivity',\n1177\t            'tau_s': 'Baseline Time Constant',\n1178\t            'fresnel_decay': 'Fresnel Weight Decay',\n1179\t            'n_subcarriers': 'Subcarrier Count'\n1180\t        };\n1181\t        return names[key] || key;\n1182\t    }\n1183\t\n1184\t    // ===== Post-Feedback Explanations =====\n1185\t\n1186\t    /**\n1187\t     * Show explanation after false positive feedback\n1188\t     */\n1189\t    function showFeedbackExplanation(eventData) {\n1190\t        if (!eventData || !eventData.explainability) {\n1191\t            return;\n1192\t        }\n1193\t\n1194\t        const explanation = eventData.explainability;\n1195\t        const contributingLinks = explanation.contributing_links || [];\n1196\t        const diagnosis = explanation.diagnosis || null;\n1197\t\n1198\t        // Find the primary contributing link\n1199\t        const primaryLink = contributingLinks.length > 0 ? contributingLinks[0] : null;\n1200\t\n1201\t        let explanationText = '';\n1202\t\n1203\t        if (primaryLink) {\n1204\t            const linkName = formatLinkID(primaryLink.link_id);\n1205\t            const deltaRMS = primaryLink.delta_rms?.toFixed(4) || 'N/A';\n1206\t            const threshold = 0.02; // Standard threshold\n1207\t            const ratio = (primaryLink.delta_rms / threshold).toFixed(1);\n1208\t\n1209\t            explanationText = `The system detected motion here because: <strong>${linkName}</strong>'s signal (deltaRMS: ${deltaRMS}) exceeded the motion threshold by <strong>${ratio}x</strong>.`;\n1210\t\n1211\t            // Add root cause from diagnostic if available\n1212\t            if (diagnosis) {\n1213\t                explanationText += `<br><br><strong>Possible cause:</strong> ${diagnosis.detail}`;\n1214\t\n1215\t                if (diagnosis.advice) {\n1216\t                    explanationText += `<br><strong>What to do:</strong> ${diagnosis.advice}`;\n1217\t                }\n1218\t                explanationText += `<br><br><em>We've noted this and will apply corrections.</em>`;\n1219\t            } else {\n1220\t                explanationText += `<br><br><strong>Possible cause:</strong> Ambient RF interference or environmental changes. We've noted this and will apply corrections.`;\n1221\t            }\n1222\t        } else {\n1223\t            explanationText = 'The system detected motion based on signal patterns across multiple links. We\\'ve noted this feedback to improve accuracy.';\n1224\t        }\n1225\t\n1226\t        // Create explanation element\n1227\t        const explanationDiv = document.createElement('div');\n1228\t        explanationDiv.className = 'feedback-explanation';\n1229\t        explanationDiv.innerHTML = `\n1230\t            <div class=\"explanation-header\">\n1231\t                <span class=\"explanation-title\">Why did this happen?</span>\n1232\t            </div>\n1233\t            <div class=\"explanation-content\">\n1234\t                <p>${explanationText}</p>\n1235\t                ${contributingLinks.length > 1 ? `<p class=\"explanation-additional-links\">Contributing links: ${contributingLinks.map(l => formatLinkID(l.link_id)).join(', ')}</p>` : ''}\n1236\t            </div>\n1237\t        `;\n1238\t\n1239\t        return explanationDiv;\n1240\t    }\n1241\t\n1242\t    /**\n1243\t     * Fetch diagnostic info for a link at a specific time\n1244\t     */\n1245\t    function fetchDiagnosticForLink(linkID, timestamp) {\n1246\t        // Using the correct endpoint: /api/diagnostics/link/{linkID}?timestamp={ms}\n1247\t        return fetch(`/api/diagnostics/link/${encodeURIComponent(linkID)}?timestamp=${timestamp}`)\n1248\t            .then(res => {\n1249\t                if (!res.ok) {\n1250\t                    throw new Error(`HTTP ${res.status}: ${res.statusText}`);\n1251\t                }\n1252\t                return res.json();\n1253\t            })\n1254\t            .catch(err => {\n1255\t                console.error('Failed to fetch diagnostic:', err);\n1256\t                return null;\n1257\t            });\n1258\t    }\n1259\t\n1260\t    // ===== Helpers =====\n1261\t\n1262\t    function formatLinkID(linkID) {\n1263\t        if (!linkID) {\n1264\t            return 'Unknown Link';\n1265\t        }\n1266\t        // Format MAC address pairs nicely\n1267\t        const parts = linkID.split(':');\n1268\t        if (parts.length === 2) {\n1269\t            const mac1 = parts[0].substring(0, 8); // First 8 chars of first MAC\n1270\t            const mac2 = parts[1].substring(0, 8); // First 8 chars of second MAC\n1271\t            return `${mac1} → ${mac2}`;\n1272\t        }\n1273\t        return linkID.substring(0, 16) + '...';\n1274\t    }\n1275\t\n1276\t    // ===== Public API =====\n1277\t    window.Proactive = {\n1278\t        // Quality monitoring\n1279\t        monitorLinkQuality: monitorLinkQuality,\n1280\t      // Initial check\n2255\t        checkFeatureNotifications();\n2256\t\n2257\t        featureNotificationCheckInterval = setInterval(() => {\n2258\t            checkFeatureNotifications();\n2259\t     if (featureNotificationCheckInterval) {\n2267\t            clearInterval(featureNotificationCheckInterval);\n2268\t            featureNotificationCheckInterval = null;\n2269\t        }\n2270\t    }\n2271\t\n2272\t    /**\n2273\t     * Check for new feature discovery notifications\n2274\t     */\n2275\t    async function checkFeatureNotifications() {\n2276\t        try {\n2277\t      if (!pulsingAnimationID) {\n                pulsingAnimationID = requestAnimationFrame(animatePulse);\n                return;\n            }\n\n            pulseTime += 0.016; // Approximately    const windowMs = 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000; // 24 hours\n\n        // Initialize history for this setting if needed\n        if (!settingChangeHistory[settingKey]) {\n settingChangeHistory[settingKey] || [];\n        if (changes.length >= 3) {\n            // Show the hint\n            showSettingChangeHint(settingKey);\n
